<?php
ini_set('display_errors', 0);
ini_set('log_errors', 1);
ini_set('error_log', __DIR__ . '/php_errors.log');

ob_start();

require_once 'config.php';
require_once 'helper_functions.php';

if (session_status() === PHP_SESSION_NONE) {
    session_start();
}

header('Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8');

try {
    file_put_contents(__DIR__ . "/debug_action.txt", "\n===== NOVI POZIV " . date("Y-m-d H:i:s") . " =====\n", FILE_APPEND);
    file_put_contents(__DIR__ . "/debug_action.txt", "POST:\n" . print_r($_POST, true) . "\n", FILE_APPEND);

    if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] !== 'POST') {
        ob_clean();
        echo json_encode(['success' => false, 'message' => 'POST zahtjev potreban.']);
        exit;
    }

    // BAZE
    $mysqli = new mysqli("localhost", "srajf", "Passw0rd", "ocpp_system");
    $mysqli->set_charset("utf8mb4");

    $sim = new mysqli("localhost", "srajf", "Passw0rd", "ocpp_simulator");
    $sim->set_charset("utf8mb4");

    if ($mysqli->connect_error || $sim->connect_error) {
        throw new Exception('Greška pri spajanju na bazu.');
    }

    // LOGIN
    requireLogin();
    file_put_contents(__DIR__ . "/debug_action.txt", "AFTER requireLogin\n", FILE_APPEND);

    $uid    = intval($_SESSION['user_id'] ?? 0);
    $id     = intval($_POST['id'] ?? 0);
    $action = trim($_POST['action'] ?? '');

    $allowedActions = ['start','pause','stop','plug_in','unplug'];
    if ($id === 0 || !in_array($action, $allowedActions, true)) {
        ob_clean();
        echo json_encode(['success' => false, 'message' => 'Nevažeci podaci.']);
        exit;
    }

    // PRAVA
    $allowed = false;

    if (isAdminSystem($uid)) {
        $allowed = true;
    } elseif (hasRight($uid, 'Administrator ustanove')) {
        $stmt = $mysqli->prepare("
            SELECT 1 FROM Punionica p
            JOIN Korisnik k ON k.ID_Ustanove = p.ID_Ustanove
            WHERE p.ID = ? AND k.ID = ? LIMIT 1
        ");
        $stmt->bind_param('ii', $id, $uid);
        $stmt->execute();
        $allowed = (bool)$stmt->get_result()->fetch_row();
    } else {
        $stmt = $mysqli->prepare("
            SELECT ImaPravo FROM Pristup_Punionici
            WHERE ID_Punionice = ? AND ID_Korisnika = ? LIMIT 1
        ");
        $stmt->bind_param('ii', $id, $uid);
        $stmt->execute();
        $r = $stmt->get_result()->fetch_assoc();
        $allowed = ($r && intval($r['ImaPravo']) === 1);
    }

    file_put_contents(__DIR__ . "/debug_action.txt", "AFTER RIGHTS CHECK allowed=" . ($allowed ? '1' : '0') . "\n", FILE_APPEND);

    if (!$allowed) {
        ob_clean();
        echo json_encode(['success' => false, 'message' => 'Nema pristupa punionici.']);
        exit;
    }

    // PLUG STATE
    $plugState = $sim->query("
        SELECT plugged_in 
        FROM connector_state
        WHERE chargepoint_id = $id AND connector_id = 1
        ORDER BY last_update DESC, id DESC
        LIMIT 1
    ")->fetch_assoc();

    $isPlugged = $plugState ? intval($plugState['plugged_in']) : 0;

    file_put_contents(__DIR__ . "/debug_action.txt", "CURRENT PLUG STATE: $isPlugged\n", FILE_APPEND);

    // PLUG IN
    if ($action === 'plug_in') {

        $sql = "INSERT INTO connector_state (chargepoint_id, connector_id, plugged_in, last_update)
                VALUES ($id, 1, 1, NOW())";

        $sim->query($sql);

        file_put_contents(__DIR__ . "/debug_action.txt", "PLUG_IN SQL: $sql\n", FILE_APPEND);

        exec("php -q /var/www/ocpp-php/src/Examples/v16/status_Preparing.php > /dev/null 2>&1 &");

        // KLJUCNI FIX
        ob_clean();

        echo json_encode(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Kabel uštekan.']);
        exit;
    }

    // UNPLUG
    if ($action === 'unplug') {

        $sql = "INSERT INTO connector_state (chargepoint_id, connector_id, plugged_in, last_update)
                VALUES ($id, 1, 0, NOW())";

        $sim->query($sql);

        file_put_contents(__DIR__ . "/debug_action.txt", "UNPLUG SQL: $sql\n", FILE_APPEND);

        exec("php -q /var/www/ocpp-php/src/Examples/v16/status_Available.php > /dev/null 2>&1 &");

        ob_clean();
        echo json_encode(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Kabel izvaden.']);
        exit;
    }

    // START
    if ($action === 'start' && $isPlugged === 0) {
        ob_clean();
        echo json_encode(['success' => false, 'message' => 'Auto nije uštekan.']);
        exit;
    }

    $map = [
        'start' => 'RemoteStartTransaction',
        'pause' => 'PauseCharging',
        'stop'  => 'RemoteStopTransaction'
    ];

    $naredba   = $map[$action];
    $parametar = null;

    if ($action === 'pause') {
        exec("php -q /var/www/ocpp-php/src/Examples/v16/status_SuspendedEVSE.php > /dev/null 2>&1 &");
        ob_clean();
    }

    if ($action === 'stop') {
        exec("php -q /var/www/ocpp-php/src/Examples/v16/status_Finishing.php > /dev/null 2>&1 &");
        ob_clean();
    }

    if ($action === 'start') {
        exec("php -q /var/www/ocpp-php/src/Examples/v16/status_Charging.php > /dev/null 2>&1 &");
        ob_clean();
    }

    // UPIS U NAREDBE
    $stmt = $mysqli->prepare("
        INSERT INTO Naredbe (ID_Punionice, Naredba, Parametar, Id_status, Vrijeme)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, 1, NOW())
    ");
    $stmt->bind_param('sss', $id, $naredba, $parametar);
    $stmt->execute();

    ob_clean();
    echo json_encode(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Naredba upisana.']);

} catch (Throwable $e) {

    file_put_contents(__DIR__ . "/debug_action.txt", "EXCEPTION: " . $e->getMessage() . "\n", FILE_APPEND);

    ob_clean();
    echo json_encode(['success' => false, 'message' => 'Greška: ' . $e->getMessage()]);
}

===== NOVI POZIV 2026-01-25 20:04:10 =====
POST:
Array
